import { StateCreator } from 'zustand';
import { GamePart } from '@/features/kanji-core/types';

// UIä¸Šã§ã®ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„å‹ï¼ˆã‚°ãƒªãƒƒãƒ‰ç‰ˆï¼‰
export interface PartState extends GamePart {
  gridIndex: number; // 0 ~ 15 (4x4ã®å ´åˆ)
}

// ä»®åˆä½“ï¼ˆãƒ—ãƒ¬ãƒ“ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ï¼‰ã®çŠ¶æ…‹
export interface PendingMergeState {
  sourceId: string;    // å…ƒã®ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„ï¼ˆæ‰‹æœ­ï¼‰
  targetId: string;    // åˆä½“å…ˆã®ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„ï¼ˆå ´ã®ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„ï¼‰
  previewChar: string; // åˆä½“å¾Œã®äºˆæ¸¬æ¼¢å­—ï¼ˆä¾‹ï¼š"æ˜"ï¼‰
}

export interface PartsSlice {
  parts: PartState[];
  selectedPartId: string | null;     // é¸æŠä¸­ã®ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„ID
  pendingMerge: PendingMergeState | null; // ä»®åˆä½“ä¸­ã®æƒ…å ±

  setParts: (parts: PartState[]) => void;
  selectPart: (id: string | null) => void;
  setPendingMerge: (state: PendingMergeState | null) => void;
  
  // ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„ç§»å‹•ï¼ˆã‚°ãƒªãƒƒãƒ‰é–“ç§»å‹•ã‚„åˆä½“ç¢ºå®šæ™‚ï¼‰
  movePart: (id: string, toIndex: number) => void;
  removePart: (id: string) => void;
  addPart: (part: PartState) => void;
}

export const createPartsSlice: StateCreator<PartsSlice> = (set) => ({
  parts: [],
  selectedPartId: null,
  pendingMerge: null,
  
  setParts: (parts) => set({ parts, selectedPartId: null, pendingMerge: null }),
  
  selectPart: (id) => set({ selectedPartId: id }),
  
  setPendingMerge: (state) => set({ pendingMerge: state }),

  movePart: (id, toIndex) => 
    set((state) => ({
      parts: state.parts.map((p) => 
        p.id === id ? { ...p, gridIndex: toIndex } : p
      ),
    })),

  removePart: (id) => 
    set((state) => ({
      parts: state.parts.filter((p) => p.id !== id),
    })),

  addPart: (part) => 
    set((state) => ({
      parts: [...state.parts, part],
    })),
});--- src/features/game-board/stores/slices/stageSlice.ts ---
import { StateCreator } from 'zustand';
import { JukugoDefinition } from '@/features/kanji-core/types';

// â–¼ è¿½åŠ 
export type DifficultyMode = 'EASY' | 'NORMAL';

export interface StageSlice {
  levelIndex: number;
  maxReachedLevel: number;
  currentJukugo: JukugoDefinition | null;
  isCleared: boolean;
  filledIndices: number[];
  historyIds: string[];
  difficultyMode: DifficultyMode; // â–¼ è¿½åŠ 

  setLevelIndex: (index: number) => void;
  setStage: (jukugo: JukugoDefinition) => void;
  setCleared: (cleared: boolean) => void;
  checkAndFillSlot: (char: string) => boolean;
  resetStage: () => void;
  setDifficultyMode: (mode: DifficultyMode) => void; // â–¼ è¿½åŠ 
}

export const createStageSlice: StateCreator<StageSlice> = (set, get) => ({
  levelIndex: 0,
  maxReachedLevel: 0,
  currentJukugo: null,
  isCleared: false,
  filledIndices: [],
  historyIds: [],
  difficultyMode: 'NORMAL', // â–¼ åˆæœŸå€¤ã¯NORMALã«ã—ã¦ãŠãã¾ã™

  setLevelIndex: (index) => set({ levelIndex: index }),

  // ... (setStage, setCleared, checkAndFillSlot ã¯å¤‰æ›´ãªã—) ...
  setStage: (jukugo) => {
    const { historyIds } = get();
    const newHistory = [...historyIds, jukugo.id].slice(-50);
    set({ 
      currentJukugo: jukugo, 
      isCleared: false, 
      filledIndices: [],
      historyIds: newHistory
    });
  },

  setCleared: (cleared) => {
    const state = get();
    if (cleared) {
      if (state.levelIndex >= state.maxReachedLevel) {
        set({ isCleared: cleared, maxReachedLevel: state.levelIndex + 1 });
        return;
      }
    }
    set({ isCleared: cleared });
  },

  checkAndFillSlot: (char) => {
    const state = get();
    if (!state.currentJukugo) return false;

    const targetIndex = state.currentJukugo.components.findIndex(
      (c, idx) => c === char && !state.filledIndices.includes(idx)
    );

    if (targetIndex !== -1) {
      const newFilled = [...state.filledIndices, targetIndex];
      set({ filledIndices: newFilled });
      if (newFilled.length === state.currentJukugo.components.length) {
        get().setCleared(true);
      }
      return true;
    }
    return false;
  },

  resetStage: () => set({ isCleared: false, filledIndices: [] }),

  // â–¼ è¿½åŠ 
  setDifficultyMode: (mode) => set({ difficultyMode: mode }),
});--- src/features/game-board/stores/store.ts ---
// src/features/game-board/stores/store.ts

import { create } from 'zustand';
import { persist } from 'zustand/middleware';
import { PartsSlice, createPartsSlice } from './slices/partsSlice';
import { StageSlice, createStageSlice } from './slices/stageSlice';
import { DictionarySlice, createDictionarySlice } from '@/features/dictionary/stores/dictionarySlice'; // ãƒ‘ã‚¹ã¯ç’°å¢ƒã«åˆã‚ã›ã¦ãã ã•ã„
import { EffectSlice, createEffectSlice } from './slices/effectSlice';
import { ThemeSlice, createThemeSlice } from './slices/themeSlice';

// â–¼ å‹å®šç¾©ã«è¿½åŠ : resetSaveData ã‚’å«ã‚ã‚‹
type GameStore = PartsSlice & StageSlice & DictionarySlice & EffectSlice & ThemeSlice & {
  resetSaveData: () => void;
};

export const useGameStore = create<GameStore>()(
  persist(
    (...a) => ({
      ...createPartsSlice(...a),
      ...createStageSlice(...a),
      // ã‚‚ã— createDictionarySlice ã®å¼•æ•°ã‚„å‹ãŒåˆã‚ãªã„å ´åˆã¯èª¿æ•´ã—ã¦ãã ã•ã„
      // åŸºæœ¬çš„ã«ã¯ ...a (set, get, api) ã‚’æ¸¡ã›ã°OKã§ã™
      ...createDictionarySlice(...a), 
      ...createEffectSlice(...a),
      ...createThemeSlice(...a),

      // â–¼ è¿½åŠ : ãƒªã‚»ãƒƒãƒˆæ©Ÿèƒ½ã®å®Ÿè£…
      resetSaveData: () => {
        // 1. ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒ¬ãƒ¼ã‚¸ã‚’å‰Šé™¤
        localStorage.removeItem('kanji-merge-storage');
        
        // 2. ãƒšãƒ¼ã‚¸ã‚’ãƒªãƒ­ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã—ã¦ã€å¼·åˆ¶çš„ã«åˆæœŸçŠ¶æ…‹ï¼ˆãƒ‡ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ«ãƒˆå€¤ï¼‰ã§å†é–‹ã•ã›ã‚‹
        // (stateã‚’å€‹åˆ¥ã«setã§æˆ»ã™ã‚ˆã‚Šã€ã“ã‚ŒãŒä¸€ç•ªç¢ºå®Ÿã§ãƒã‚°ãŒèµ·ãã«ãã„ã§ã™)
        window.location.reload();
      },
    }),
    {
      name: 'kanji-merge-storage',
      partialize: (state) => ({ 
        unlockedIds: state.unlockedIds,
        unlockedJukugos: state.unlockedJukugos,
        // levelIndex ã‚„ maxReachedLevel ãªã©ã€StageSliceã®ãƒ—ãƒ­ãƒ‘ãƒ†ã‚£åã«åˆã‚ã›ã¦ãã ã•ã„
        // StageSliceã®å®šç¾©ã«ã‚ˆã‚Šã¾ã™ãŒã€æã‚‰ã currentLevel ãªã©ã‚’ä¿å­˜ã—ã¦ã„ã‚‹ã¯ãšã§ã™
        levelIndex: state.levelIndex, 
        maxReachedLevel: state.maxReachedLevel,
        historyIds: state.historyIds, 
        currentTheme: state.currentTheme,
      }),
    }
  )
);--- src/features/game-board/hooks/useGridInteraction.ts ---
import { useGameStore } from "../stores/store";
import { judgeMerge } from "@/features/kanji-core/logic/merger";
import { getConstituents } from "@/features/kanji-core/logic/decomposer"; // è¿½åŠ 
import { soundEngine } from "@/lib/sounds/SoundEngine";

export function useGridInteraction() {
  const parts = useGameStore((state) => state.parts);
  const selectedPartId = useGameStore((state) => state.selectedPartId);
  const selectPart = useGameStore((state) => state.selectPart);
  
  const pendingMerge = useGameStore((state) => state.pendingMerge);
  const setPendingMerge = useGameStore((state) => state.setPendingMerge);
  
  const movePart = useGameStore((state) => state.movePart);
  const removePart = useGameStore((state) => state.removePart);
  const addPart = useGameStore((state) => state.addPart);
  const checkAndFillSlot = useGameStore((state) => state.checkAndFillSlot);
  const unlockKanji = useGameStore((state) => state.unlockKanji);
  const unlockJukugo = useGameStore((state) => state.unlockJukugo);
  const currentJukugo = useGameStore((state) => state.currentJukugo);

  // ç¢ºå®šå‡¦ç†ï¼ˆåˆä½“ï¼‰
  const confirmMerge = () => {
    if (!pendingMerge) return;

    soundEngine.playGoal(); // æ±ºå®šéŸ³
    unlockKanji(pendingMerge.previewChar);
    removePart(pendingMerge.sourceId);
    removePart(pendingMerge.targetId);

    // 1. ã‚´ãƒ¼ãƒ«åˆ¤å®š
    const isGoal = checkAndFillSlot(pendingMerge.previewChar);
    
    if (isGoal) {
      soundEngine.playGoal();
      if (useGameStore.getState().isCleared && currentJukugo) {
        unlockJukugo(currentJukugo.id);
      }
    } else {
      // 2. ã‚´ãƒ¼ãƒ«ã˜ã‚ƒãªã„ã‘ã©åˆä½“æˆåŠŸï¼ˆç›¤é¢ã«ç½®ãï¼‰
      // åˆä½“å…ˆã®ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„ä½ç½®ã‚’å–å¾—
      const targetPart = parts.find(p => p.id === pendingMerge.targetId);
      if (targetPart) {
        addPart({
          id: Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 9),
          char: pendingMerge.previewChar,
          type: "KANJI",
          gridIndex: targetPart.gridIndex,
        });
      }
    }

    setPendingMerge(null);
    selectPart(null);
  };

  // åˆ†è§£å‡¦ç†
  const handleSplit = (partId: string) => {
    const targetPart = parts.find(p => p.id === partId);
    if (!targetPart) return;

    // æ§‹æˆãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„ã‚’å–å¾—
    const constituents = getConstituents(targetPart.char);
    if (!constituents) return; // åˆ†è§£ã§ããªã„æ–‡å­—

    // ç©ºããƒã‚¹ã‚’æ¢ã™ï¼ˆåˆ†è§£ã™ã‚‹ã¨ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„ãŒ1ã¤å¢—ãˆã‚‹ãŸã‚ã€1ã¤ç©ºããŒå¿…è¦ï¼‰
    // ç¾åœ¨ã®ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„ãŒã„ãŸå ´æ‰€(1) + ç©ºããƒã‚¹(1) = è¨ˆ2ãƒã‚¹å¿…è¦
    const occupiedIndices = parts.map(p => p.gridIndex);
    // 4x4=16ãƒã‚¹ã¨ä»®å®š (storeã§å®šæ•°åŒ–ã™ã¹ãã ãŒä¸€æ—¦ãƒã‚¸ãƒƒã‚¯ãƒŠãƒ³ãƒãƒ¼)
    const gridSize = 16;
    let emptyIndex = -1;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < gridSize; i++) {
      if (!occupiedIndices.includes(i)) {
        emptyIndex = i;
        break;
      }
    }

    if (emptyIndex === -1) {
      // ç©ºããŒãªã„ã®ã§åˆ†è§£ä¸å¯ï¼ˆã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼éŸ³ãªã©é³´ã‚‰ã™ã¨è‰¯ã„ï¼‰
      return;
    }

    // åˆ†è§£å®Ÿè¡Œ
    soundEngine.playSelect(); // åˆ†è§£éŸ³ï¼ˆä»®ï¼‰
    removePart(targetPart.id);
    
    // ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„Aã‚’å…ƒã®ä½ç½®ã«
    addPart({
      id: Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 9),
      char: constituents[0],
      type: "RADICAL", // ä¾¿å®œä¸ŠRADICALã«æˆ»ã™ï¼ˆå®Ÿéš›ã¯KANJIã‹ã‚‚ã ãŒï¼‰
      gridIndex: targetPart.gridIndex,
    });
    
    // ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„Bã‚’ç©ºãä½ç½®ã«
    addPart({
      id: Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 9),
      char: constituents[1],
      type: "RADICAL",
      gridIndex: emptyIndex,
    });

    selectPart(null);
  };

  const handleSlotClick = (index: number) => {
    soundEngine.init();

    // --- A. ä»®åˆä½“ä¸­ï¼ˆãƒ—ãƒ¬ãƒ“ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ä¸­ï¼‰ ---
    if (pendingMerge) {
      const targetPart = parts.find(p => p.id === pendingMerge.targetId);
      if (targetPart && targetPart.gridIndex === index) {
        confirmMerge(); // ç¢ºå®š
        return;
      }
      setPendingMerge(null);
      // ã‚­ãƒ£ãƒ³ã‚»ãƒ«ã—ã¦é€šå¸¸å‡¦ç†ã¸
    }

    // --- B. é€šå¸¸æ™‚ ---
    const clickedPart = parts.find((p) => p.gridIndex === index);

    // â˜… ã‚¯ãƒªãƒƒã‚¯ã—ãŸãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„ãŒã‚´ãƒ¼ãƒ«å¯¾è±¡ãªã‚‰å³å›åï¼ˆã“ã‚Œã¯ç¶­æŒï¼‰
    if (clickedPart) {
      const isSelfTap = clickedPart.id === selectedPartId;
      if (!isSelfTap) {
        const isGoal = checkAndFillSlot(clickedPart.char);
        if (isGoal) {
          soundEngine.playGoal();
          removePart(clickedPart.id);
          selectPart(null);
          if (useGameStore.getState().isCleared && currentJukugo) {
            unlockJukugo(currentJukugo.id);
          }
          return;
        }
      }
    }

    // 1. ä½•ã‚‚é¸æŠã—ã¦ã„ãªã„æ™‚
    if (!selectedPartId) {
      if (clickedPart) {
        selectPart(clickedPart.id);
      }
      return;
    }

    // 2. é¸æŠä¸­ã€åŒã˜ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„ã‚’ã‚¿ãƒƒãƒ— â†’ â˜…åˆ†è§£åˆ¤å®šâ˜…
    if (clickedPart && clickedPart.id === selectedPartId) {
      // é¸æŠä¸­ã®ã‚‚ã®ã‚’ã‚‚ã†ä¸€åº¦ã‚¿ãƒƒãƒ—ã—ãŸã‚‰åˆ†è§£ã‚’è©¦ã¿ã‚‹
      const constituents = getConstituents(clickedPart.char);
      if (constituents) {
        handleSplit(clickedPart.id);
      } else {
        // åˆ†è§£ã§ããªã„ãªã‚‰é¸æŠè§£é™¤
        selectPart(null);
      }
      return;
    }

    const sourcePart = parts.find((p) => p.id === selectedPartId);
    if (!sourcePart) {
      selectPart(null);
      return;
    }

    // 3. ç©ºããƒã‚¹ã¸ç§»å‹•
    if (!clickedPart) {
      movePart(sourcePart.id, index);
      selectPart(null);
      return;
    }

    // 4. åˆ¥ã®ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„ã¨åˆä½“åˆ¤å®š
    if (clickedPart) {
      const result = judgeMerge(sourcePart.char, clickedPart.char);

      if (result.success && result.newChar) {
        setPendingMerge({
          sourceId: sourcePart.id,
          targetId: clickedPart.id,
          previewChar: result.newChar,
        });
        soundEngine.playMerge();
      } else {
        selectPart(clickedPart.id);
      }
    }
  };

  return { handleSlotClick };
}--- src/features/game-board/hooks/useLevelSystem.ts ---
import { useEffect, useCallback, useRef } from "react";
import { useGameStore } from "../stores/store";
import { generateRandomStage } from "@/features/kanji-core/logic/generator";
import { generateStageParts } from "@/features/kanji-core/logic/decomposer";

export function useLevelSystem() {
  const currentLevelIndex = useGameStore((state) => state.levelIndex);
  // â˜…è¿½åŠ : ç¾åœ¨ã®é›£æ˜“åº¦ãƒ¢ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã‚’ç›£è¦–
  const difficultyMode = useGameStore((state) => state.difficultyMode);

  const setLevelIndex = useGameStore((state) => state.setLevelIndex);
  const setParts = useGameStore((state) => state.setParts);
  const setStage = useGameStore((state) => state.setStage);
  const resetStage = useGameStore((state) => state.resetStage);
  
  const loadedLevelRef = useRef<number | null>(null);
  // â˜…è¿½åŠ : ãƒ­ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã—ãŸæ™‚ã®ãƒ¢ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã‚‚è¨˜éŒ²ã—ã¦ãŠãï¼ˆãƒ¢ãƒ¼ãƒ‰åˆ‡æ›¿æ™‚ã®å†ãƒ­ãƒ¼ãƒ‰åˆ¤å®šç”¨ï¼‰
  const loadedModeRef = useRef<string | null>(null);

  const loadLevel = useCallback((index: number) => {
    // ã‚¹ãƒˆã‚¢ã‹ã‚‰ç›´æ¥æœ€æ–°ã®çŠ¶æ…‹ã‚’å–å¾—
    const state = useGameStore.getState();
    const currentHistoryIds = state.historyIds;
    // â˜…è¿½åŠ : ãƒ¢ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã‚’å–å¾—
    const mode = state.difficultyMode;

    // â˜…ä¿®æ­£: ç¬¬3å¼•æ•°ã« mode ã‚’æ¸¡ã™
    const jukugoDef = generateRandomStage(index, currentHistoryIds, mode);

    console.log(`ğŸ“¥ Loading Level ${index + 1} [${mode}]: ${jukugoDef.kanji} (Diff: ${jukugoDef.difficulty})`);

    resetStage();
    setStage(jukugoDef);

    // â˜…ä¿®æ­£: ç¬¬3å¼•æ•°ã« mode ã‚’æ¸¡ã™
    const initialParts = generateStageParts(jukugoDef, index, mode);
    setParts(initialParts as any);
    
    loadedLevelRef.current = index;
    loadedModeRef.current = mode; // â˜…è¨˜éŒ²
  }, [setParts, setStage, resetStage]); 

  useEffect(() => {
    // ãƒ¬ãƒ™ãƒ«ãŒå¤‰ã‚ã£ãŸã€ã¾ãŸã¯ãƒ¢ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ãŒå¤‰ã‚ã£ãŸå ´åˆã«ãƒ­ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã‚’å®Ÿè¡Œ
    if (
      loadedLevelRef.current === currentLevelIndex && 
      loadedModeRef.current === difficultyMode
    ) {
      return;
    }
    
    loadLevel(currentLevelIndex);
  }, [currentLevelIndex, difficultyMode, loadLevel]); // â˜…difficultyMode ã‚’ä¾å­˜é…åˆ—ã«è¿½åŠ 

  const nextLevel = () => {
    setLevelIndex(currentLevelIndex + 1);
  };

  return {
    currentLevelIndex,
    nextLevel,
    reloadLevel: () => loadLevel(currentLevelIndex)
  };
}--- src/features/game-board/constants/themes.ts ---

    sub: string;            // è£œè¶³æ–‡å­—è‰²
    partBg: string;         // ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„ã®èƒŒæ™¯
    partBorder: string;     // ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ãƒ„ã®æ ç·š
    slotBg: string;         // ã‚´ãƒ¼ãƒ«ã‚¹ãƒ­ãƒƒãƒˆã®èƒŒæ™¯
    slotBorder: string;     // ã‚´ãƒ¼ãƒ«ã‚¹ãƒ­ãƒƒãƒˆã®æ 
  };
}

      background: 'bg-[#2b4033]', // æ·±ç·‘

      accent: 'text-[#facc15]',   // ãƒãƒ§ãƒ¼ã‚¯ã®é»„è‰²
      sub: 'text-stone-300',
      partBg: 'bg-[#1a2e22]',
      partBorder: 'border-stone-400',
      slotBg: 'bg-white/10',
      slotBorder: 'border-white/30',
    },
  },
  cyber: {
    id: 'cyber',
    name: 'é›»è„³',
    colors: {
      background: 'bg-[#0f172a]', // æ¿ƒã„ç´º
      text: 'text-[#22d3ee]',     // ãƒã‚ªãƒ³ã‚·ã‚¢ãƒ³
      accent: 'text-[#f472b6]',   // ãƒã‚ªãƒ³ãƒ”ãƒ³ã‚¯

      partBg: 'bg-[#1e293b]',
      partBorder: 'border-[#22d3ee]/50',
      slotBg: 'bg-[#1e293b]/50',

};--- src/lib/sounds/SoundEngine.ts ---
/**
 * ç°¡æ˜“ã‚·ãƒ³ã‚»ã‚µã‚¤ã‚¶ãƒ¼ã‚¨ãƒ³ã‚¸ãƒ³ (Enhanced)
 * MP3ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ãªã—ã§ã€BGMã‚„ç’°å¢ƒéŸ³ã‚‚ç”Ÿæˆã—ã¾ã™ã€‚
 */
class SoundEngine {
  private ctx: AudioContext | null = null;
  private isMuted: boolean = false;
  private currentAmbience: AudioNode[] = []; // å†ç”Ÿä¸­ã®ç’°å¢ƒéŸ³ãƒãƒ¼ãƒ‰

  constructor() {
    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
      const AudioContextClass = window.AudioContext || (window as any).webkitAudioContext;
      if (AudioContextClass) {
        this.ctx = new AudioContext();
      }
    }
  }

  public init() {
    if (this.ctx && this.ctx.state === 'suspended') {
      this.ctx.resume();
    }
  }

  // --- åŸºæœ¬æ³¢å½¢ç”Ÿæˆ ---
  private playTone(freq: number, type: OscillatorType, duration: number, startTime: number = 0, vol: number = 0.3) {
    if (!this.ctx || this.isMuted) return;

    const osc = this.ctx.createOscillator();
    const gain = this.ctx.createGain();

    osc.type = type;
    osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(freq, this.ctx.currentTime + startTime);

    gain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, this.ctx.currentTime + startTime);
    gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(vol, this.ctx.currentTime + startTime + 0.01);
    gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, this.ctx.currentTime + startTime + duration);

    osc.connect(gain);
    gain.connect(this.ctx.destination);

    osc.start(this.ctx.currentTime + startTime);
    osc.stop(this.ctx.currentTime + startTime + duration);
  }

  // --- ãƒã‚¤ã‚ºç”Ÿæˆ (ç’°å¢ƒéŸ³ç”¨) ---
  private createNoiseBuffer(): AudioBuffer | null {
    if (!this.ctx) return null;
    const bufferSize = this.ctx.sampleRate * 2; // 2ç§’åˆ†
    const buffer = this.ctx.createBuffer(1, bufferSize, this.ctx.sampleRate);
    const data = buffer.getChannelData(0);
    for (let i = 0; i < bufferSize; i++) {
      data[i] = Math.random() * 2 - 1;
    }
    return buffer;
  }

  // --- ã‚¢ãƒ³ãƒ“ã‚¨ãƒ³ã‚¹å†ç”Ÿ ---
  
  public stopAmbience() {
    this.currentAmbience.forEach(node => {
      try { (node as any).stop(); } catch(e) {}
      node.disconnect();
    });
    this.currentAmbience = [];
  }

  // é¢¨ã®éŸ³ (æ£®ãƒ»å±±ã‚¨ãƒªã‚¢ç”¨)
  public playWindAmbience() {
    if (!this.ctx || this.isMuted) return;
    this.stopAmbience();

    const noise = this.ctx.createBufferSource();
    noise.buffer = this.createNoiseBuffer();
    noise.loop = true;

    // ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ã§é¢¨ã®ã‚ˆã†ãªã‚´ã‚©ãƒ¼ã¨ã„ã†éŸ³ã«ã™ã‚‹
    const filter = this.ctx.createBiquadFilter();
    filter.type = 'lowpass';
    filter.frequency.value = 400;
    
    // éŸ³é‡æºã‚‰ã (LFO)
    const lfo = this.ctx.createOscillator();
    lfo.type = 'sine';
    lfo.frequency.value = 0.2; // ã‚†ã£ãŸã‚Š
    const lfoGain = this.ctx.createGain();
    lfoGain.gain.value = 300; // ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿å‘¨æ³¢æ•°ã‚’æºã‚‰ã™

    const mainGain = this.ctx.createGain();
    mainGain.gain.value = 0.05; // ã‹ãªã‚Šå°ã•ã

    lfo.connect(lfoGain);
    lfoGain.connect(filter.frequency);
    
    noise.connect(filter);
    filter.connect(mainGain);
    mainGain.connect(this.ctx.destination);

    noise.start();
    lfo.start();

    this.currentAmbience.push(noise, lfo);
  }

  // å·ã®ã›ã›ã‚‰ã (é‡Œã‚¨ãƒªã‚¢ç”¨)
  public playRiverAmbience() {
    if (!this.ctx || this.isMuted) return;
    this.stopAmbience();

    const noise = this.ctx.createBufferSource();
    noise.buffer = this.createNoiseBuffer();
    noise.loop = true;

    // ãƒã‚¤ãƒ‘ã‚¹ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ã§ã‚·ãƒ£ãƒ¯ã‚·ãƒ£ãƒ¯æ„Ÿ
    const filter = this.ctx.createBiquadFilter();
    filter.type = 'highpass';
    filter.frequency.value = 800;

    const mainGain = this.ctx.createGain();
    mainGain.gain.value = 0.03;

    noise.connect(filter);
    filter.connect(mainGain);
    mainGain.connect(this.ctx.destination);

    noise.start();
    this.currentAmbience.push(noise);
  }

  // å®‡å®™ã®é™å¯‚ (å¤©ç©ºã‚¨ãƒªã‚¢ç”¨)
  public playSpaceAmbience() {
    if (!this.ctx || this.isMuted) return;
    this.stopAmbience();

    // ä½ã„ãƒ‰ãƒ­ãƒ¼ãƒ³éŸ³
    const osc = this.ctx.createOscillator();
    osc.type = 'sine';
    osc.frequency.value = 50; // è¶…ä½éŸ³

    const lfo = this.ctx.createOscillator();
    lfo.frequency.value = 0.1;
    const lfoGain = this.ctx.createGain();
    lfoGain.gain.value = 10; 

    const mainGain = this.ctx.createGain();
    mainGain.gain.value = 0.1;

    lfo.connect(lfoGain);
    lfoGain.connect(osc.frequency);
    osc.connect(mainGain);
    mainGain.connect(this.ctx.destination);

    osc.start();
    lfo.start();
    this.currentAmbience.push(osc, lfo);
  }

  // --- SEãƒ—ãƒªã‚»ãƒƒãƒˆ ---

  public playMerge() {
    this.init();
    this.playTone(880, 'square', 0.1); 
    this.playTone(440, 'triangle', 0.1); 
  }

  public playGoal() {
    this.init();
    this.playTone(1200, 'sine', 0.3);
    this.playTone(1800, 'sine', 0.3, 0.1); 
  }

  public playStamp() {
    this.init();
    // ä½ã„ãƒ‰ãƒ³ãƒƒã¨ã„ã†éŸ³
    this.playTone(150, 'triangle', 0.15, 0, 0.8);
    // ç´™ã®æ‘©æ“¦éŸ³ã£ã½ã„ãƒã‚¤ã‚ºï¼ˆç°¡æ˜“ï¼‰
    this.playTone(800, 'square', 0.05, 0, 0.1);
  }

  public playClear() {
    this.init();
    const now = 0;
    this.playTone(523.25, 'triangle', 0.5, now);       // ãƒ‰
    this.playTone(659.25, 'triangle', 0.5, now + 0.1); // ãƒŸ
    this.playTone(783.99, 'triangle', 0.5, now + 0.2); // ã‚½
    this.playTone(1046.50, 'sine', 0.8, now + 0.3);    // é«˜ã„ãƒ‰
  }

  public playSelect() {
    this.init();
    // çŸ­ãé«˜ã„éŸ³ã§ã€Œã‚³ãƒƒã€ã¨ã„ã†æ„Ÿã˜
    this.playTone(800, 'square', 0.05, 0, 0.1);
  }
}

export const soundEngine = new SoundEngine();--- src/lib/utils/tw-merge.ts ---
import { type ClassValue, clsx } from "clsx";
import { twMerge } from "tailwind-merge";

export function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {
  return twMerge(clsx(inputs));
}
